In-Shape March Lane is a well equipted, well maintained, affordable workout and spa facility. Always well staffed, this staff is always polite, helpful and actively serving members. This is a no airs environment with abundant ethnic, age, and physical attribute diversity among its friendly membership. A gender sinsitivity is evident by a female only workout space. The 24 hour weekday schedule  allows me access to this fine facility for under 80 cents a day. This also includes a clean pool, hot spa, sauna and steam room. Great showers and locker rooms. Great bargain.< /Review>

<Review>Finally joined Inshape after so many years, thoughts, and consideration. I was near the location so I thought I swing on by, prior to joining Inshape on Aug 16 2018 since I've got a good deal through my workplace corp discount. The facility itself was big, but the only reason why I gave it 3-stars was due to the lack of exercise equipment available. This location didn't have much workout machines for my LE which was kind of disappointing, or unless I must've missed it somewhere, but I do wished there was more of the free-weighted smith machine squat racks available. Not a big fan of the assisted smith machines. Nonetheless, I enjoyed the circuit training area, which has enough space to get some bodyweight exercises in but still lack certain circuit machine. I can utilize the floor drawings and be creative with my workout so that made it fun and educate my muscles and body with the work of some therapeutic exercises. I love TRX and they provide that at this facility which I can do all sorts of fun workout with it. The facility itself was A-Ok, just wish they had more available LE machine. I had to finished the rest of my LE workout at 24hrs Fitness, which is another gym I have for a long time, but that is another review on their Yelp and Google review page. Overall, the layout of the gym is clean and nice, but this will probably be my least favorite Inshape location, I'll probably use this location for a good cardio with racquetball. I will just stick to Quails and Bianchi, or probably Hammer too.</Review>< userid>

< text>
All of the staff is kind, patient, and thorough. Dr. Baldwin is a great surgeon and took great care of my son. My son had all 4 impacted wisdom teeth removed, drilling into the jaw for removal. They hadn't erputed yet, but the roots were growing dangerously close to his nerves. Surgery went easier than expected with less trauma than anticipated, as she was able remove the teeth whole. His post-op care was wonderful as well, with Dr. Baldwin personally checking in, and she was easily reachable after hours when my son had a slight complication. Dr. Baldwin identified a medical condition my son may have, and we went to his primary care office for testing. We're still awaiting tests there, but are grateful Dr. Baldwin is so sharp and knowledgeable to have identified this and let us know. The doctor and staff truly made the whole process easier. I'll give 3 tips: 1) Ask for extra of the wax/plastic bags the ice packs go in; you'll put ziplock bags of ice into those bags. Ours didn't last more than 12 hours. 2) Ask for a couple extra of the bands that hold the ice packs in place, they lose their stretch quickly. 3) Make sure to fill all prescriptions in advance, and follow all instructions exactly; ask questions if you have any as you go along.</text>

This is a fantastic place for breakfast prices are extremely reasonable. I've eaten at the Oak Pit Steakhouse in Porterville and the steaks at the Cow puncher are by far better. When you're driving by it looks like a little hole in the wall the floors are not level and the tables look like they are about 60 years old. Don't let that fool you the food is fantastic. I would definitely recommend this place if you are driving by or anywhere near the area I would drive up from Porterville just to eat there it's only about 15 minutes from Porterville.< /text>
